     â•‘  HOW TO ADD A NEW HOTSPOT:                                     â•‘
     â•‘  1. Copy a START/END block below                               â•‘

     â•‘  3. Change label (display name)                                â•‘

<script>

/* â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•
   REGIONS â€” Add/edit regions here
   Key = internal id, label = display name
   â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â• */
const REGIONS = {
  andes:     { label: "Andes", order: 1 },
  caribe:    { label: "Caribe", order: 2 },
  pacifico:  { label: "PacÃ­fico", order: 3 },
  amazonia:  { label: "AmazonÃ­a", order: 4 },
  orinoquia: { label: "OrinoquÃ­a", order: 5 },
};


/* â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•

/* â•â•â• DOM REFS â•â•â• */
const pagesRoot   = document.getElementById('pages-root');
const measureRoot  = document.getElementById('measure-root');
const template     = document.getElementById('header-template');
const emptyState   = document.getElementById('emptyState');
const statusBar    = document.getElementById('statusBar');
const statusMsg    = document.getElementById('statusMsg');
const statusPages  = document.getElementById('statusPages');
const toast        = document.getElementById('toast');
const toastMsg     = document.getElementById('toastMsg');
const toastIcon    = document.getElementById('toastIcon');

const BLOCK_SPACING = 9;
const SAFETY_BUFFER = 12;
let mergedData = [];
let showScientific = true;

const esc = (s) => s ? s.replace(/&/g,'&amp;').replace(/</g,'&lt;').replace(/>/g,'&gt;') : '';

/* â•â•â• TOAST â•â•â• */
let toastTimer;
function showToast(msg, type = 'success') {
  clearTimeout(toastTimer);
  toastMsg.innerHTML = msg;
  toastIcon.className = `toast-icon ${type}`;
  toastIcon.innerHTML = type === 'success'
    ? '<svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2.5"><polyline points="20 6 9 17 4 12"/></svg>'
    : '<svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2.5"><line x1="18" y1="6" x2="6" y2="18"/><line x1="6" y1="6" x2="18" y2="18"/></svg>';
  toast.classList.add('show');
  toastTimer = setTimeout(() => toast.classList.remove('show'), 4000);
}


/* â•â•â• NORMALIZE for dedup â•â•â• */
function normSci(s) {
  return (s || '').trim().toLowerCase()
    .normalize('NFD').replace(/[\u0300-\u036f]/g, '')
    .replace(/\s+/g, ' ');
}


/* â•â•â• BUILD SIDEBAR â•â•â• */
function buildSidebar() {
  const container = document.getElementById('hotspotList');

  // Group hotspots by region
  const byRegion = {};
  HOTSPOTS.forEach(h => {
    if (!byRegion[h.region]) byRegion[h.region] = [];
    byRegion[h.region].push(h);
  });

  // Sort regions by order
  const regionKeys = Object.keys(byRegion).sort((a, b) =>
    (REGIONS[a]?.order || 99) - (REGIONS[b]?.order || 99)
  );

  container.innerHTML = '';

  regionKeys.forEach(rk => {
    const reg = REGIONS[rk] || { label: rk };
    const hotspots = byRegion[rk];

    const group = document.createElement('div');
    group.className = 'region-group';
    group.dataset.region = rk;

    group.innerHTML = `
      <div class="region-header">
        <svg class="region-arrow" width="12" height="12" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="3"><polyline points="6 9 12 15 18 9"/></svg>
        <span>${esc(reg.label)}</span>
        <span class="region-count">${hotspots.length} hotspot${hotspots.length > 1 ? 's' : ''}</span>
      </div>
      <div class="region-hotspots">
        ${hotspots.map(h => `
          <div class="hotspot-item" data-id="${h.id}" data-label="${esc(h.label.toLowerCase())}">
            <input type="checkbox" id="hs_${h.id}" value="${h.id}" />
            <label for="hs_${h.id}">${esc(h.label)}</label>
            <span class="hotspot-spp">${h.species.length}</span>
          </div>
        `).join('')}
      </div>
    `;

    // Toggle region collapse
    group.querySelector('.region-header').addEventListener('click', () => {
      group.classList.toggle('collapsed');
    });

    container.appendChild(group);
  });

  // Wire up checkbox changes
  container.querySelectorAll('input[type="checkbox"]').forEach(cb => {
    cb.addEventListener('change', updateStats);
  });
}


/* â•â•â• SEARCH FILTER â•â•â• */
document.getElementById('hotspotSearch').addEventListener('input', function() {
  const q = this.value.trim().toLowerCase();
  document.querySelectorAll('.hotspot-item').forEach(item => {
    const match = !q || item.dataset.label.includes(q);
    item.classList.toggle('hidden', !match);
  });
  // Show regions that have visible items
  document.querySelectorAll('.region-group').forEach(g => {
    const visibleItems = g.querySelectorAll('.hotspot-item:not(.hidden)');
    g.style.display = visibleItems.length ? '' : 'none';
    if (q && visibleItems.length) g.classList.remove('collapsed');
  });
});


/* â•â•â• STATS UPDATE â•â•â• */
function updateStats() {
  const selected = getSelectedIds();
  const btnGen = document.getElementById('btnGenerate');
  btnGen.disabled = selected.length === 0;

  // Compute merged stats
  let totalRows = 0;
  const seen = new Map();
  const families = new Set();

  selected.forEach(id => {
    const h = HOTSPOTS.find(x => x.id === id);
    if (!h) return;
    totalRows += h.species.length;
    h.species.forEach(([fam, eng, sci]) => {
      const key = normSci(sci);
      if (!seen.has(key)) {
        seen.set(key, true);
        families.add(fam);
      }
    });
  });

  document.getElementById('statHotspots').textContent = selected.length;
  document.getElementById('statRows').textContent = totalRows;
  document.getElementById('statUnique').textContent = seen.size;
  document.getElementById('statFamilies').textContent = families.size;

  // Sync mobile FAB and toggle count
  if (typeof syncFab === 'function') syncFab();
}

function getSelectedIds() {
  return Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('#hotspotList input[type="checkbox"]:checked'))
    .map(cb => cb.value);
}


/* â•â•â• MERGE + DEDUPE â•â•â• */
function mergeHotspots(selectedIds) {
  const seen = new Map();
  const result = [];

  selectedIds.forEach(id => {
    const h = HOTSPOTS.find(x => x.id === id);
    if (!h) return;
    h.species.forEach(([fam, eng, sci]) => {
      const key = normSci(sci);
      if (!seen.has(key)) {
        seen.set(key, true);
        result.push({ eng: eng.trim(), sci: sci.trim(), fam: fam.trim() });
      }
    });
  });

  return result;
}

function groupByFamily(species) {
  const groups = {};
  const seen = new Set();

  species.forEach(s => {
    if (!groups[s.fam]) { groups[s.fam] = []; seen.add(s.fam); }
    groups[s.fam].push({ eng: s.eng, sci: s.sci });
  });

  // Sort by taxonomic order; families not in the list go at the end alphabetically
  const famIndex = {};
  FAMILY_ORDER.forEach((f, i) => { famIndex[f] = i; });

  const order = Array.from(seen).sort((a, b) => {
    const ia = famIndex[a] !== undefined ? famIndex[a] : 9999;
    const ib = famIndex[b] !== undefined ? famIndex[b] : 9999;
    if (ia !== ib) return ia - ib;
    return a.localeCompare(b);
  });

  return { groups, order };
}


/* â•â•â• BUILD BLOCK (for page rendering) â•â•â• */
function buildBlock(famName, birds, showContinued) {
  const headerText = showContinued
    ? `${esc(famName)} <span class="cont-label">(cont.)</span>`
    : esc(famName);
  let listHtml = '';
  birds.forEach(b => {
    if (!b.eng || !b.eng.trim()) return;
    const sciHtml = (showScientific && b.sci) ? `<span class="species-sci">${esc(b.sci)}</span>` : '';
    listHtml += `<div class="species-item"><span class="checkbox"></span><div style="flex:1;line-height:1.25;"><span class="species-name">${esc(b.eng)}</span>${sciHtml}</div></div>`;
  });
  return `<div class="family-block"><div class="family-header">${headerText}</div><hr class="family-divider"/>${listHtml}</div>`;
}


/* â•â•â• CREATE PAGE â•â•â• */
function createPageElement(isFirst) {
  const page = document.createElement('div');
  page.className = 'sheet';
  const headerContent = template.content.cloneNode(true);
  const headerDiv = document.createElement('div');
  headerDiv.appendChild(headerContent);

  // Logo â†’ absolute in page
  const logoImg = headerDiv.querySelector('.header-logo');
  if (logoImg) {
    logoImg.src = LOGO_SVG;
    logoImg.style.display = document.getElementById('toggleLogo')?.checked ? 'block' : 'none';
    headerDiv.querySelector('.header-logo')?.remove();
    page.appendChild(logoImg);
  }

  if (!isFirst) {
    headerDiv.querySelector('.header-fields')?.remove();
    headerDiv.querySelector('.checklist-note')?.remove();
    headerDiv.querySelector('.legal-text')?.remove();
    headerDiv.querySelector('.header-hr')?.remove();
    const note = document.createElement('div');
    note.className = 'continued-note';
    note.textContent = '\u2014 Checklist Continued \u2014';
    headerDiv.appendChild(note);
    const divider = document.createElement('hr');
    divider.className = 'continued-divider';
    headerDiv.appendChild(divider);
  } else {
    if (!document.getElementById('toggleFooter')?.checked) {
      const lt = headerDiv.querySelector('.legal-text');
      const hr = headerDiv.querySelector('.header-hr');
      if (lt) lt.style.display = 'none';
      if (hr) hr.style.display = 'none';
    }
    if (!document.getElementById('toggleNote')?.checked) {
      const cn = headerDiv.querySelector('.checklist-note');
      if (cn) cn.style.display = 'none';
    }
  }

  // Watermark
  const wm = document.createElement('div');
  wm.className = 'watermark';
  if (document.getElementById('toggleWatermark')?.checked) wm.classList.add('visible');
  wm.innerHTML = '<img src="' + LOGO_SVG + '" alt="" />';
  page.appendChild(wm);

  const ca = document.createElement('div');
  ca.className = 'checklist-area';
  ca.innerHTML = '<div class="cols"><div class="col" data-idx="0"></div><div class="col" data-idx="1"></div><div class="col" data-idx="2"></div></div>';
  page.appendChild(headerDiv);
  page.appendChild(ca);
  return { page, checklistArea: ca };
}

function getColWidth(pageEl) { return pageEl.querySelector('.col').getBoundingClientRect().width; }

function measureHtml(html, width) {
  measureRoot.style.width = width + 'px';
  measureRoot.innerHTML = html;
  return measureRoot.offsetHeight + BLOCK_SPACING;
}


/* â•â•â• GENERATE PAGES â•â•â• */
async function generatePages() {
  pagesRoot.innerHTML = '';
  if (!mergedData.length) return;

  // Temporarily neutralize mobile zoom so getBoundingClientRect returns true sizes
  const sheetsNeedZoomReset = window.innerWidth <= 1024;
  if (sheetsNeedZoomReset) {
    pagesRoot.style.zoom = '1';
    pagesRoot.style.transform = 'none';
  }

  const { groups, order } = groupByFamily(mergedData);

  let cur = createPageElement(true);
  pagesRoot.appendChild(cur.page);
  // Force zoom:1 on the sheet itself during measurement
  cur.page.style.zoom = '1';
  cur.page.style.transform = 'none';
  await new Promise(r => requestAnimationFrame(r));

  let colWidth = getColWidth(cur.page);
  let maxH = cur.checklistArea.getBoundingClientRect().height - SAFETY_BUFFER;
  let cols = Array.from(cur.page.querySelectorAll('.col'));
  let colH = [0, 0, 0];
  let ci = 0;

  const nextCol = () => { ci++; if (ci > 2) nextPage(); };
  const nextPage = () => {
    cur = createPageElement(false);
    pagesRoot.appendChild(cur.page);
    cur.page.style.zoom = '1';
    cur.page.style.transform = 'none';
    cols = Array.from(cur.page.querySelectorAll('.col'));
    colH = [0, 0, 0]; ci = 0;
    maxH = cur.checklistArea.getBoundingClientRect().height - SAFETY_BUFFER;
  };
  const addBlock = (html, h) => { cols[ci].insertAdjacentHTML('beforeend', html); colH[ci] += h; };

  for (const fam of order) {
    const allBirds = groups[fam];
    let rem = [...allBirds];
    let first = true;

    while (rem.length > 0) {
      const avail = maxH - colH[ci];
      const fHtml = buildBlock(fam, rem, !first);
      const fH = measureHtml(fHtml, colWidth);

      if (fH <= avail) { addBlock(fHtml, fH); rem = []; }
      else if (fH <= maxH) { nextCol(); const nh = buildBlock(fam, rem, !first); addBlock(nh, measureHtml(nh, colWidth)); rem = []; }
      else {
        let lo = 1, hi = rem.length, best = 1;
        while (lo <= hi) {
          const mid = Math.floor((lo + hi) / 2);
          if (measureHtml(buildBlock(fam, rem.slice(0, mid), !first), colWidth) <= avail) { best = mid; lo = mid + 1; }
          else { hi = mid - 1; }
        }
        if (best === 0 || (best === 1 && avail < 80)) { nextCol(); continue; }
        const bHtml = buildBlock(fam, rem.slice(0, best), !first);
        addBlock(bHtml, measureHtml(bHtml, colWidth));
        rem = rem.slice(best);
        first = false;
      }
      if (first && rem.length < allBirds.length) first = false;
    }
  }

  // Restore: remove inline zoom overrides so CSS zoom kicks back in
  if (sheetsNeedZoomReset) {
    pagesRoot.style.removeProperty('zoom');
    pagesRoot.style.removeProperty('transform');
    pagesRoot.querySelectorAll('.sheet').forEach(s => {
      s.style.removeProperty('zoom');
      s.style.removeProperty('transform');
    });
  }
}


/* â•â•â• GENERATE BUTTON â•â•â• */
async function doGenerate() {
  const selected = getSelectedIds();
  if (!selected.length) return;

  mergedData = mergeHotspots(selected);
  await document.fonts.ready;
  await generatePages();

  // Apply dynamic zoom on mobile
  applyMobileZoom();

  const familyCount = new Set(mergedData.map(s => s.fam)).size;
  const pageCount = document.querySelectorAll('.sheet').length;

  statusBar.classList.add('visible');
  statusMsg.textContent = `âœ“ ${mergedData.length} especies Ãºnicas Â· ${familyCount} familias`;
  statusPages.textContent = `${pageCount} pÃ¡gina(s)`;

  emptyState.style.display = 'none';
  document.getElementById('btnPrint').disabled = false;

  // Update mobile FAB
  syncFab();

  showToast(`<strong>${mergedData.length}</strong> especies de <strong>${selected.length}</strong> hotspots`);

  // On mobile: collapse sidebar and scroll to results
  if (window.innerWidth <= 768) {
    const sidebar = document.getElementById('sidebar');
    sidebar.classList.add('collapsed');
    updateToggleCount();
    setTimeout(() => {
      document.querySelector('.toggle-bar').scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'start' });
    }, 400);
  }
}

document.getElementById('btnGenerate').addEventListener('click', doGenerate);


/* â•â•â• CLEAR BUTTON â•â•â• */
function doClear() {
  document.querySelectorAll('#hotspotList input[type="checkbox"]').forEach(cb => cb.checked = false);
  mergedData = [];
  pagesRoot.innerHTML = '';
  emptyState.style.display = '';
  statusBar.classList.remove('visible');
  document.getElementById('btnPrint').disabled = true;
  updateStats();
  syncFab();
  showToast('SelecciÃ³n limpiada', 'success');
}
document.getElementById('btnClear').addEventListener('click', doClear);


/* â•â•â• PRINT / SAVE PDF â•â•â• */
function doPrint() {
  if (!mergedData.length) { showToast('Genera el checklist primero', 'error'); return; }

  const inIframe = window.self !== window.top;
  const mobile = isMobile();

  // On mobile or inside iframe (Wix), open a new tab with print-ready content
  if (mobile || inIframe) {
    showToast('Preparando PDFâ€¦', 'success');

    // Collect sheet HTML
    const sheets = document.querySelectorAll('.sheet');
    let sheetsHtml = '';
    sheets.forEach(s => {
      // Clone without inline zoom styles
      const clone = s.cloneNode(true);
      clone.style.cssText = '';
      sheetsHtml += clone.outerHTML;
    });

    // Build standalone print document
    const printDoc = `<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="es">
<head>
<meta charset="UTF-8">
<meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0">

<style>
:root {
  --ink-900: #1a1a1a; --ink-700: #3d3d3d; --ink-500: #6b6b6b;

  --btn-green: #678100;
}
*, *::before, *::after { box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0; padding: 0; }
body { background: #f3f4f6; margin: 0; padding: 0; font-family: 'Montserrat', sans-serif; }

.sheet {
  background: white; width: 8.5in; height: 11in;
  margin: 0 auto; padding: 0.45in 0.5in 0.55in 0.5in;
  box-sizing: border-box; position: relative; overflow: hidden;
  display: flex; flex-direction: column;
  border-top: 3px solid var(--btn-green);
}
.checklist-area { flex: 1; overflow: hidden; position: relative; z-index: 1; }

.family-block { margin-bottom: 9px; width: 100%; page-break-inside: avoid; break-inside: avoid; }

.species-name { font-weight: 700; color: var(--ink-900); }
.species-sci { font-style: italic; font-weight: 400; color: var(--ink-500); margin-left: 3px; font-size: 9px; }
.continued-note { font-family: 'Montserrat', sans-serif; font-size: 8.5px; font-weight: 400; color: var(--ink-300); margin-top: -6px; margin-bottom: 4px; text-align: center; font-style: italic; letter-spacing: 0.04em; }
.continued-divider { border: none; border-bottom: 1px dashed var(--ink-200); margin: 0 0 6px 0; height: 0; }

${sheetsHtml}

  // Auto-trigger print after short delay for fonts
  setTimeout(() => { try { window.print(); } catch(e) {} }, 600);

<\/script>
</body></html>`;

    const blob = new Blob([printDoc], { type: 'text/html' });
    const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
    const w = window.open(url, '_blank');

    if (!w) {
      // Popup blocked â€” try direct link
      const a = document.createElement('a');
      a.href = url;
      a.target = '_blank';
      a.rel = 'noopener';
      a.click();
    }

    // Cleanup after delay
    setTimeout(() => URL.revokeObjectURL(url), 60000);

  } else {
    // Desktop, not in iframe â€” direct print
    window.print();
  }
}
document.getElementById('btnPrint').addEventListener('click', doPrint);

/* Safety net: force inline resets for any print trigger (Ctrl+P, browser menu, etc.) */
window.addEventListener('beforeprint', () => {
  document.querySelectorAll('.sheet').forEach(s => {
    s.style.setProperty('transform', 'none', 'important');
    s.style.setProperty('-webkit-transform', 'none', 'important');
    s.style.setProperty('zoom', '1', 'important');
    s.style.setProperty('margin-bottom', '0', 'important');
    s.style.setProperty('margin-top', '0', 'important');
    s.style.setProperty('width', '8.5in', 'important');
    s.style.setProperty('height', '11in', 'important');
  });
});
window.addEventListener('afterprint', () => {
  document.querySelectorAll('.sheet').forEach(s => {
    ['transform', '-webkit-transform', 'zoom', 'margin-bottom', 'margin-top', 'width', 'height']
      .forEach(p => s.style.removeProperty(p));
  });
  // Restore mobile zoom after print
  if (isMobile() && mergedData.length) applyMobileZoom();
});


/* â•â•â• TOGGLE HANDLERS â•â•â• */
function reapplyToggles() {
  const fc = document.getElementById('toggleFooter').checked;
  document.querySelectorAll('.legal-text').forEach(el => el.style.display = fc ? 'block' : 'none');
  document.querySelectorAll('.header-hr').forEach(el => el.style.display = fc ? 'block' : 'none');
  const nc = document.getElementById('toggleNote').checked;
  document.querySelectorAll('.checklist-note').forEach(el => el.style.display = nc ? 'block' : 'none');
  const lc = document.getElementById('toggleLogo').checked;
  document.querySelectorAll('.header-logo').forEach(el => el.style.display = lc ? 'block' : 'none');
  const wc = document.getElementById('toggleWatermark').checked;
  document.querySelectorAll('.watermark').forEach(el => { if (wc) el.classList.add('visible'); else el.classList.remove('visible'); });
}

document.getElementById('toggleFooter').addEventListener('change', reapplyToggles);
document.getElementById('toggleNote').addEventListener('change', reapplyToggles);
document.getElementById('toggleLogo').addEventListener('change', reapplyToggles);
document.getElementById('toggleWatermark').addEventListener('change', reapplyToggles);

document.getElementById('toggleSci').addEventListener('change', async function() {
  showScientific = this.checked;
  if (mergedData.length) {
    await generatePages();
    applyMobileZoom();
    reapplyToggles();
  }
});


/* â•â•â• MOBILE: Sidebar toggle, FAB sync, dynamic zoom â•â•â• */
function isMobile() { return window.innerWidth <= 768; }

function updateToggleCount() {
  const el = document.getElementById('sidebarToggleCount');
  if (!el) return;
  const n = getSelectedIds().length;
  el.textContent = n > 0 ? `${n} seleccionado${n > 1 ? 's' : ''}` : '';
}

function syncFab() {
  const fabGen = document.getElementById('fabGenerate');
  const fabPrt = document.getElementById('fabPrint');
  const fabStat = document.getElementById('fabStatus');
  if (!fabGen) return;

  const selected = getSelectedIds();
  fabGen.disabled = selected.length === 0;
  fabPrt.disabled = !mergedData.length;

  if (mergedData.length) {
    fabStat.textContent = `${mergedData.length} spp Â· ${document.querySelectorAll('.sheet').length}p`;
  } else if (selected.length) {
    fabStat.textContent = `${selected.length} hotspot${selected.length > 1 ? 's' : ''}`;
  } else {
    fabStat.textContent = '';
  }
  updateToggleCount();
}

function applyMobileZoom() {
  // Dynamic zoom: fit sheet width to viewport
  if (!isMobile()) return;
  const vw = window.innerWidth;
  const sheetW = 8.5 * 96; // 816px at 96dpi
  const targetZoom = Math.min((vw - 16) / sheetW, 0.52); // 8px padding each side
  document.querySelectorAll('.sheet').forEach(s => {
    s.style.zoom = targetZoom;
  });
}

// Sidebar collapse toggle
document.getElementById('sidebarToggle').addEventListener('click', () => {
  const sidebar = document.getElementById('sidebar');
  sidebar.classList.toggle('collapsed');
});

// FAB Generate button mirrors main Generate
document.getElementById('fabGenerate').addEventListener('click', doGenerate);

// FAB Print button mirrors main Print
document.getElementById('fabPrint').addEventListener('click', doPrint);

// On resize, reapply mobile zoom
window.addEventListener('resize', () => {
  if (mergedData.length) applyMobileZoom();
});

// Start sidebar collapsed on mobile if no hotspots are selected
if (isMobile()) {
  // Will be open by default so user sees hotspots to select
}

buildSidebar();
updateStats();

/* â•â•â• VALIDATION (check console for errors) â•â•â• */
(function validateData() {
  const errors = [];
  const allIds = new Set();
  HOTSPOTS.forEach((h, i) => {
    if (!h.id) errors.push(`Hotspot[${i}]: falta "id"`);
    if (allIds.has(h.id)) errors.push(`Hotspot "${h.id}": id DUPLICADO`);
    allIds.add(h.id);
    if (!h.label) errors.push(`Hotspot "${h.id}": falta "label"`);
    if (!REGIONS[h.region]) errors.push(`Hotspot "${h.id}": region "${h.region}" no existe en REGIONS`);
    if (!Array.isArray(h.species)) errors.push(`Hotspot "${h.id}": "species" no es un array`);
    else {
      h.species.forEach(([fam, eng, sci], j) => {
        if (!eng) errors.push(`Hotspot "${h.id}" especie[${j}]: falta English Name`);
        if (!sci) errors.push(`Hotspot "${h.id}" especie[${j}]: falta Scientific Name â€” "${eng}"`);
        if (!fam) errors.push(`Hotspot "${h.id}" especie[${j}]: falta Family â€” "${eng}"`);
      });
    }
  });
  if (errors.length) {
    console.error(`ğŸ¦ VALIDACIÃ“N: ${errors.length} error(es):`);
    errors.forEach(e => console.error('  âŒ ' + e));
  } else {
    console.log(`ğŸ¦ VALIDACIÃ“N OK: ${HOTSPOTS.length} hotspots, ${HOTSPOTS.reduce((s,h)=>s+h.species.length,0)} filas totales`);
  }
})();

document.fonts.ready.then(() => console.log('Montserrat loaded'));
</script>
